\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00075}00075 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00076}00076 \textcolor{comment}{// Limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00077}00077 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no jpeg progressive support}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00078}00078 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ non-\/HDR formats support 8-\/bit samples only (jpeg, png)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00079}00079 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no delayed line count (jpeg) -\/-\/ IJG doesn't support either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00080}00080 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ no 1-\/bit BMP}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00081}00081 \textcolor{comment}{//    -\/ GIF always returns *comp=4}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00082}00082 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00083}00083 \textcolor{comment}{// Basic usage (see HDR discussion below):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00084}00084 \textcolor{comment}{//    int x,y,n;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00085}00085 \textcolor{comment}{//    unsigned char *data = stbi\_load(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00086}00086 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... process data if not NULL ... }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00087}00087 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... x = width, y = height, n = \# 8-\/bit components per pixel ...}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00088}00088 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... replace '0' with '1'..'4' to force that many components per pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00089}00089 \textcolor{comment}{//    // ... but 'n' will always be the number that it would have been if you said 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00090}00090 \textcolor{comment}{//    stbi\_image\_free(data)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00091}00091 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00092}00092 \textcolor{comment}{// Standard parameters:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00093}00093 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *x       -\/-\/ outputs image width in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00094}00094 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *y       -\/-\/ outputs image height in pixels}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00095}00095 \textcolor{comment}{//    int *comp    -\/-\/ outputs \# of image components in image file}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00096}00096 \textcolor{comment}{//    int req\_comp -\/-\/ if non-\/zero, \# of image components requested in result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00097}00097 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00098}00098 \textcolor{comment}{// The return value from an image loader is an 'unsigned char *' which points}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00099}00099 \textcolor{comment}{// to the pixel data. The pixel data consists of *y scanlines of *x pixels,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00100}00100 \textcolor{comment}{// with each pixel consisting of N interleaved 8-\/bit components; the first}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00101}00101 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel pointed to is top-\/left-\/most in the image. There is no padding between}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00102}00102 \textcolor{comment}{// image scanlines or between pixels, regardless of format. The number of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00103}00103 \textcolor{comment}{// components N is 'req\_comp' if req\_comp is non-\/zero, or *comp otherwise.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00104}00104 \textcolor{comment}{// If req\_comp is non-\/zero, *comp has the number of components that \_would\_}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00105}00105 \textcolor{comment}{// have been output otherwise. E.g. if you set req\_comp to 4, you will always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00106}00106 \textcolor{comment}{// get RGBA output, but you can check *comp to easily see if it's opaque.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00107}00107 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00108}00108 \textcolor{comment}{// An output image with N components has the following components interleaved}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00109}00109 \textcolor{comment}{// in this order in each pixel:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00110}00110 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00111}00111 \textcolor{comment}{//     N=\#comp     components}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00112}00112 \textcolor{comment}{//       1           grey}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00113}00113 \textcolor{comment}{//       2           grey, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00114}00114 \textcolor{comment}{//       3           red, green, blue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00115}00115 \textcolor{comment}{//       4           red, green, blue, alpha}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00116}00116 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00117}00117 \textcolor{comment}{// If image loading fails for any reason, the return value will be NULL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00118}00118 \textcolor{comment}{// and *x, *y, *comp will be unchanged. The function stbi\_failure\_reason()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00119}00119 \textcolor{comment}{// can be queried for an extremely brief, end-\/user unfriendly explanation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00120}00120 \textcolor{comment}{// of why the load failed. Define STBI\_NO\_FAILURE\_STRINGS to avoid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00121}00121 \textcolor{comment}{// compiling these strings at all, and STBI\_FAILURE\_USERMSG to get slightly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00122}00122 \textcolor{comment}{// more user-\/friendly ones.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00123}00123 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00124}00124 \textcolor{comment}{// Paletted PNG, BMP, GIF, and PIC images are automatically depalettized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00125}00125 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00126}00126 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00127}00127 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00128}00128 \textcolor{comment}{// iPhone PNG support:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00129}00129 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00130}00130 \textcolor{comment}{// By default we convert iphone-\/formatted PNGs back to RGB; nominally they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00131}00131 \textcolor{comment}{// would silently load as BGR, except the existing code should have just}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00132}00132 \textcolor{comment}{// failed on such iPhone PNGs. But you can disable this conversion by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00133}00133 \textcolor{comment}{// by calling stbi\_convert\_iphone\_png\_to\_rgb(0), in which case}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00134}00134 \textcolor{comment}{// you will always just get the native iphone "{}format"{} through.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00135}00135 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00136}00136 \textcolor{comment}{// Call stbi\_set\_unpremultiply\_on\_load(1) as well to force a divide per}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00137}00137 \textcolor{comment}{// pixel to remove any premultiplied alpha *only* if the image file explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00138}00138 \textcolor{comment}{// says there's premultiplied data (currently only happens in iPhone images,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00139}00139 \textcolor{comment}{// and only if iPhone convert-\/to-\/rgb processing is on).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00140}00140 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00141}00141 \textcolor{comment}{// ===========================================================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00142}00142 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00143}00143 \textcolor{comment}{// HDR image support   (disable by defining STBI\_NO\_HDR)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00144}00144 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00145}00145 \textcolor{comment}{// stb\_image now supports loading HDR images in general, and currently}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00146}00146 \textcolor{comment}{// the Radiance .HDR file format, although the support is provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00147}00147 \textcolor{comment}{// generically. You can still load any file through the existing interface;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00148}00148 \textcolor{comment}{// if you attempt to load an HDR file, it will be automatically remapped to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00149}00149 \textcolor{comment}{// LDR, assuming gamma 2.2 and an arbitrary scale factor defaulting to 1;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00150}00150 \textcolor{comment}{// both of these constants can be reconfigured through this interface:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00151}00151 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00152}00152 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00153}00153 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_hdr\_to\_ldr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{// (note, do not use \_inverse\_ constants; stbi\_image will invert them}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriately).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{// Additionally, there is a new, parallel interface for loading files as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{// (linear) floats to preserve the full dynamic range:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{//    float *data = stbi\_loadf(filename, \&x, \&y, \&n, 0);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{// }}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{// If you load LDR images through this interface, those images will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{// be promoted to floating point values, run through the inverse of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{// constants corresponding to the above:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_scale(1.0f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_ldr\_to\_hdr\_gamma(2.2f);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, given a filename (or an open file or memory block-\/-\/see header}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{// file for details) containing image data, you can query for the "{}most}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{// appropriate"{} interface to use (that is, whether the image is HDR or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{// not), using:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{//     stbi\_is\_hdr(char *filename);}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{// through a small internal buffer (currently 128 bytes) to try to reduce}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00187}00187 \textcolor{comment}{// "{}skip"{} (skips some bytes of data), "{}eof"{} (reports if the stream is at the end).}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l00843}00843 \textcolor{comment}{//  generic converter from built-\/in img\_n to req\_comp}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01967}01967 \textcolor{comment}{// public domain zlib decode    v0.2  Sean Barrett 2006-\/11-\/18}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01968}01968 \textcolor{comment}{//    simple implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01969}01969 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all input must be provided in an upfront buffer}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01970}01970 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ all output is written to a single output buffer (can malloc/realloc)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01971}01971 \textcolor{comment}{//    performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01972}01972 \textcolor{comment}{//      -\/ fast huffman}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01973}01973 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01974}01974 \textcolor{comment}{// fast-\/way is faster to check than jpeg huffman, but slow way is slower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01975}01975 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define ZFAST\_BITS  9 }\textcolor{comment}{// accelerate all cases in default tables}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l01977}01977 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02483}02483    \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j=0; j < y; ++j) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02485}02485       stbi\_\_uint8 *prior = cur -\/ stride;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02488}02488       \textcolor{comment}{// if first row, use special filter that doesn't sample previous row}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02489}02489       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (j == 0) filter = first\_row\_filter[filter];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02490}02490       \textcolor{comment}{// handle first pixel explicitly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02491}02491       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (k=0; k < img\_n; ++k) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02492}02492          \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02493}02493             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_none       : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02494}02494             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_sub        : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02495}02495             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_up         : cur[k] = raw[k] + prior[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02497}02497             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_paeth      : cur[k] = (stbi\_\_uint8) (raw[k] + paeth(0,prior[k],0)); \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02498}02498             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_avg\_first  : cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02499}02499             \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} F\_paeth\_first: cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02500}02500          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02501}02501       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02502}02502       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n != out\_n) cur[img\_n] = 255;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02503}02503       raw += img\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02504}02504       cur += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02505}02505       prior += out\_n;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02506}02506       \textcolor{comment}{// this is a little gross, so that we don't switch per-\/pixel or per-\/component}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02507}02507       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (img\_n == out\_n) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02508}02508 \textcolor{preprocessor}{         \#define CASE(f) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02509}02509 \textcolor{preprocessor}{             case f:     \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02510}02510 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                for (i=x-\/1; i >= 1; -\/-\/i, raw+=img\_n,cur+=img\_n,prior+=img\_n) \(\backslash\)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02511}02511 \textcolor{preprocessor}{                   for (k=0; k < img\_n; ++k)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02512}02512          \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (filter) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02513}02513             CASE(F\_none)  cur[k] = raw[k]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l02514}02514             CASE(F\_sub)   cur[k] = raw[k] + cur[k-\/img\_n]; \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03348}03348             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( !RLE\_repeating )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03349}03349             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03350}03350                read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03351}03351             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03352}03352          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03353}03353          \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03354}03354             read\_next\_pixel = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03355}03355          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03356}03356          \textcolor{comment}{//   OK, if I need to read a pixel, do it now}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03357}03357          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( read\_next\_pixel )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03358}03358          \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03359}03359             \textcolor{comment}{//   load however much data we did have}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03360}03360             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( tga\_indexed )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03361}03361             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03362}03362                \textcolor{comment}{//   read in 1 byte, then perform the lookup}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03363}03363                \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} pal\_idx = get8u(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03364}03364                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( pal\_idx >= tga\_palette\_len )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03365}03365                \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03366}03366                   \textcolor{comment}{//   invalid index}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03367}03367                   pal\_idx = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03368}03368                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03369}03369                pal\_idx *= tga\_bits\_per\_pixel / 8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03370}03370                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j*8 < tga\_bits\_per\_pixel; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03371}03371                \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03372}03372                   raw\_data[j] = tga\_palette[pal\_idx+j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03373}03373                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03374}03374             \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03375}03375             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03376}03376                \textcolor{comment}{//   read in the data raw}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03377}03377                \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j*8 < tga\_bits\_per\_pixel; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03378}03378                \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03379}03379                   raw\_data[j] = get8u(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03380}03380                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03381}03381             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03382}03382             \textcolor{comment}{//   clear the reading flag for the next pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03383}03383             read\_next\_pixel = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03384}03384          \} \textcolor{comment}{// end of reading a pixel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03385}03385 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03386}03386          \textcolor{comment}{// copy data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03387}03387          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j < tga\_comp; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03388}03388            tga\_data[i*tga\_comp+j] = raw\_data[j];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03389}03389 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03390}03390          \textcolor{comment}{//   in case we're in RLE mode, keep counting down}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03391}03391          -\/-\/RLE\_count;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03392}03392       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03393}03393       \textcolor{comment}{//   do I need to invert the image?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03394}03394       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( tga\_inverted )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03395}03395       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03396}03396          \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (j = 0; j*2 < tga\_height; ++j)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03397}03397          \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03398}03398             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index1 = j * tga\_width * req\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03399}03399             \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index2 = (tga\_height -\/ 1 -\/ j) * tga\_width * req\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03400}03400             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = tga\_width * req\_comp; i > 0; -\/-\/i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03401}03401             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03402}03402                \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} temp = tga\_data[index1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03403}03403                tga\_data[index1] = tga\_data[index2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03404}03404                tga\_data[index2] = temp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03405}03405                ++index1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03406}03406                ++index2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03407}03407             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03408}03408          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03409}03409       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03410}03410       \textcolor{comment}{//   clear my palette, if I had one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03411}03411       \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ( tga\_palette != NULL )}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03412}03412       \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03413}03413          free( tga\_palette );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03414}03414       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03415}03415    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03416}03416 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03417}03417    \textcolor{comment}{// swap RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03418}03418    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (tga\_comp >= 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03419}03419    \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03420}03420       \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}* tga\_pixel = tga\_data;}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03426}03426          tga\_pixel += tga\_comp;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03427}03427       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03428}03428    \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03429}03429 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03432}03432       tga\_data = convert\_format(tga\_data, tga\_comp, req\_comp, tga\_width, tga\_height);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03433}03433 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03496}03496    \textcolor{comment}{// Make sure the color mode is RGB.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03497}03497    \textcolor{comment}{// Valid options are:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03500}03500    \textcolor{comment}{//   2: Indexed color}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03504}03504    \textcolor{comment}{//   8: Duotone}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03505}03505    \textcolor{comment}{//   9: Lab color}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03506}03506    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (get16(s) != 3)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03507}03507       \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} epuc(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}wrong color format"{}}, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}PSD is not in RGB color format"{}});}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03511}03511 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03512}03512    \textcolor{comment}{// Skip the image resources.  (resolution, pen tool paths, etc)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03514}03514 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03517}03517 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03518}03518    \textcolor{comment}{// Find out if the data is compressed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03522}03522    compression = get16(s);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03534}03534    \textcolor{comment}{// Finally, the image data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03535}03535    \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (compression) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03536}03536       \textcolor{comment}{// RLE as used by .PSD and .TIFF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03537}03537       \textcolor{comment}{// Loop until you get the number of unpacked bytes you are expecting:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03538}03538       \textcolor{comment}{//     Read the next source byte into n.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03539}03539       \textcolor{comment}{//     If n is between 0 and 127 inclusive, copy the next n+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03540}03540       \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is between -\/127 and -\/1 inclusive, copy the next byte -\/n+1 times.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03541}03541       \textcolor{comment}{//     Else if n is 128, noop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03542}03542       \textcolor{comment}{// Endloop}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03543}03543 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03544}03544       \textcolor{comment}{// The RLE-\/compressed data is preceeded by a 2-\/byte data count for each row in the data,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03545}03545       \textcolor{comment}{// which we're going to just skip.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03546}03546       skip(s, h * channelCount * 2 );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03547}03547 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03548}03548       \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03549}03549       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03550}03550          stbi\_\_uint8 *p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03551}03551          }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03552}03552          p = out+channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03553}03553          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel >= channelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03554}03554             \textcolor{comment}{// Fill this channel with default data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03555}03555             \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (i = 0; i < pixelCount; i++) *p = (channel == 3 ? 255 : 0), p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03556}03556          \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03557}03557             \textcolor{comment}{// Read the RLE data.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03558}03558             count = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03559}03559             \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (count < pixelCount) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03560}03560                len = get8(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03561}03561                \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len == 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03562}03562                   \textcolor{comment}{// No-\/op.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03563}03563                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len < 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03564}03564                   \textcolor{comment}{// Copy next len+1 bytes literally.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03565}03565                   len++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03566}03566                   count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03567}03567                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03568}03568                      *p = get8u(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03569}03569                      p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03570}03570                      len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03571}03571                   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03572}03572                \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (len > 128) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03573}03573                   stbi\_\_uint8   val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03574}03574                   \textcolor{comment}{// Next -\/len+1 bytes in the dest are replicated from next source byte.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03575}03575                   \textcolor{comment}{// (Interpret len as a negative 8-\/bit int.)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03576}03576                   len \string^= 0x0FF;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03577}03577                   len += 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03578}03578                   val = get8u(s);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03579}03579                   count += len;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03580}03580                   \textcolor{keywordflow}{while} (len) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03581}03581                      *p = val;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03582}03582                      p += 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03583}03583                      len-\/-\/;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03584}03584                   \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03585}03585                \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03586}03586             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03587}03587          \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03588}03588       \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03589}03589       }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03590}03590    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03591}03591       \textcolor{comment}{// We're at the raw image data.  It's each channel in order (Red, Green, Blue, Alpha, ...)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03592}03592       \textcolor{comment}{// where each channel consists of an 8-\/bit value for each pixel in the image.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03593}03593       }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03594}03594       \textcolor{comment}{// Read the data by channel.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03595}03595       \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (channel = 0; channel < 4; channel++) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03597}03597          }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03598}03598          p = out + channel;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03599}03599          \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (channel > channelCount) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{stb__image_8c_source_l03607}03607       \}}
